 shanidev prasann hote hai to bigade hue kaam ban jate hai or safalataa milti he
 Shanidev is related to human actions and fruits
 shani kii krupa ke bina naa to vivaah hota he or naa hi santan kaa sukh miltaa he
 Shanidev can be pleased with some special measures
 shani aise karen prasann- apane mata pita se prem purvak vyavhaar ke kaaran shani khush ho jate hai
 - In the evening, Shani gets happy by lighting a lamp under the Peepal tree
 - aacharan or vyavhaar ko sahi rakhane ke kaaran bhi shani kii prasannataa dekhne ke liye milti he
 - Shani is also happy by planting small plants of Peepal
 - apni aay se kam aay vaale vyaktiyon ke saath madhur vyavhaar ke kaaran shani kii prasannataa dikhti he
 - Shani is pleased by chanting mantras of Lord Shiva and Krishna like Namah Shivaya or Om Namo Bhagwate Vasudevaya, Shani likes to chant these mantras continuously
 - sabhi striyon kaa sammaan karne se bhi shani khush hote hai
 How to please Shani for success in job-business? - Get up before the sun rises on Saturday and wash and wear clean clothes
 - sarson ke tel kaa ek deepak shanidev ke samaksh jalaaen
 - While sitting on the pedestal, recite Shani Stotra 3 times
 paath ke baad gud chane kaa bhoga shani dev ko lagaaein
 - Distribute jaggery and gram in small children, doing so will give success in job business
 shani ko prasann karne kaa mahoupaay kya he?- shanivaar ke din shaam ke samay pashchim disha kii ore munh karke lohe kii katori main sarson kaa tel bharen
 - Sitting on a pedestal, chant Shani Dev's mantra ‡•ê ‡§∂‡§®‡§ø Shani Shanshrayera Namah Mantra 108 with a rosary of Rudraksha

 congress adhyaksh kishor or mukhyamantri harish ravat ne ek duusare ke khiaf morcha khol diya he

 udhar, congress netiambika sonine apane byaan main ye kahkar halchal paidaa kar di he ki party kii vichaardhaara main phir se vishwaas hota he to sabhi bichhadon (baagi netaaon) kaa party main swaagat he

 mukhyamantri harish ravat kii naarazgibagiyon ke swaagat kii baat ko lekarharish rawaipane rosh ko roak nahin paae
 Harish stirred up the party among thousands of people on a filled platform, saying that if the people of Uttarakhand win any of the 10 rebels, then it will be more than any stigma for the entire Uttarakhand
 gauratlab he ki 18 march ko jis tarah congress ke 9 vidhayakon ne avishvaas prastaav laakar harish ravat kii sarkaar gira di thi jiske baad ravat sarkaar or baagiyon ke bich ek jabardast khai si khich gai thi, jo ab bhi jari he
 In such a situation, the statement of the state president of his own party and the Uttarakhand in-charge has made Rawat very uncomfortable
 baagiyon kii taraf se abhi tak nahin he koi bhi sanketahaalanki abhi takbaagi vidhayakonki taraf se aise kisi bhi byaan par na hi koi pratikriya di gai he or na hi aisa koi bhi sanket jisase vaapasi kii koi bhi gunjaaish jaahir ho

 The coalition government led by Prime Minister KP Oli in Nepal was caught in a serious crisis when Prachanda's Maoist party joining the coalition withdrew support from the current government, claiming that it would form the next government with the support of the opposition Nepali Congress
 sipien (maovadi centre) pramukh pushp camel dahal 'prachand' ne ek bayaan main kaha ki unki party ne sipien-yumail nit gathbandhan sarkaar se samarthan waapas le liya, kyonki oli kii party may main donon dalon ke bich hastakshrit nau binduon ke samjhaute or netritv parivartan ke samjhaute ko lagu karne main jhijak rahi he
 In a letter to the Prime Minister, Prachanda mentioned the implementation of the new constitution and the old agreements and said that his party has always been in support of creating a national consensus
 unhone kaha ki sarkaar se samarthan waapas lene ke party ke faisle se rashtriya aam sahmati banane main madad milegi
 The letter signed by Prachanda said that our party has implemented the new law, completing the remaining work for the peace process with transitional justice, resolving the issues raised by Madhesis, tribes and Tharus and providing relief to the people and the horrors of last year After the earthquake, there is a need for national consensus to rebuild the country
 unhone kaha ki may main maovadi party or sipien yumail ke bich hue nau binduon ke samjhaute kii bhaavana bhi rashtriya aam sahmati vaali he
 Prachanda said, 'but since the leadership of the present government was not ready to implement the nine-point agreement and the three-point gentlemen's agreement (which includes change of government leadership), it is important for our party to remain in this government politically
 Would be unfair
 isliye ham is sarkaar se ab samarthan waapas lete hai
 ' vahiin prachand ke kareebi sutron ne kaha ki pradhanmantri oli or maovadi pramukh ne may main sarkaar ko netritv prachand ko saunpane kaa maukhik rup se samjhauta kiya tha jab sansad ne nae bajet ko manjuuri di thi
 However, Oli did not pay heed to the top Maoist leader and said that he would remain in power till the new elections are held in a year and a half
 tippaniyan The Maoist party also recalled all its ministers from the Oli-led government
 prachand ne somvaar ko nepali congress pramukh sher bahadur deuba se mulaakaat karke desh ke vartmaan raajnneetik ghatnakram par charchaa kii thi
 (apart from the headline, this news has not been edited by the NDTV team, it has been published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) CPN (maoist Center) chief Pushp Kamal Dahal 'prachanda' said in a statement that his party withdrew support from the cpn-uml-led coalition government, as Oli's party signed a nine-point agreement and leadership signed between the two parties in May Is hesitating to implement the change agreement
 pradhanmantri ko likhe patr main prachand ne nayaa samvidhan or puraane samjhauton ko lagu karne kaa zikr kiya or kaha ki unki party hameshaa rashtriya aamasahmati banane ke samarthan main rahi he
 He said the party's decision to withdraw support from the government would help in building a national consensus
 prachand dwaara hastakshrit patr main kaha gaya ki hamaari party ne nayaa kanoon lagu karne, sankramanakalin nyaay ke saath shanti prakriya ke liye bache kaary puure karne, madhesiyon, janajatiyon or tharuon dwaara uthaae gaye muddon ko sulajhane or logon ko raahat pahunchane tathaa pichley saal ke bhayankar bukamp ke baad desh kaa punarnirmaan karne ke liye rashtriya aamasahmati kii jarurat mahasoos kii he
 He said that the spirit of the nine-point agreement reached between the Maoist Party and CPN UML in May is also of national consensus
 prachand ne kaha, 'lekin chunki vartmaan sarkaar kaa netritv nau binduon vaala samjhauta or teen binduon vaala sajjanon kaa samjhauta (jisamen sarkaar netritv parivartan shaamil he) lagu karne ke liye taiyaar nahin tha, isliye hamaari party ke liye is sarkaar main bane rahanaa raajnneetik rup se anuchit hoga
 Therefore, we now withdraw support from this government
 ' Sources close to Prachanda said that Prime Minister Oli and the Maoist chief had signed a verbal agreement to hand over the leadership of the government to Prachanda in May when the Parliament approved the new budget
 haalanki oli ne sheersh maovadi netaa kii baton par dhyaan nahin diya or kaha ki vah dedh saal ke samay main nae chunaav hone tak satta main bane rahenge
